No one actually cares, they're just curious. Got a new job? Nobody cares. You passed your exams? Good job, nobody cares. What's that? You're getting married? Nobody cares. People are always curious, which isn't really a bad thing. They like to know what's going on in your life, but would they support you when you're at your lowest point in your life? No. Would they  help you when you need it most? No. There's no point telling people everything because they don't care. You have to pick yourself up and learn it the hard way. (Collected)
